『鎌倉サーキット場整備員の手記』
The Memoirs of a Maintenance Worker at the Kamakura Circuit.

一〇月三一日　第一回大和ＧＰ決勝戦　優勝　タムラ／アベンジ　二位　ヨコタン／スーパーハウンド　三位　アソシエイブル／ＲＧ-一〇ＣＸ
October 31 The First Yamato GP Final Winner: Tamura/Avenge Second: Yokotan/Super Hound Third: Assocable/RG-100CX

※終盤までレースをリードしていたのは翔京ワークスのウルティマ・シュールであったが、一九周目の第一コーナーでクラッシュ。リタイヤした。　尚、騎手は死亡。
Ultima Schurr of Shokyo Works was leading the race until the end, but crashed at the first corner on lap 19. He retired from the race.　The craft hand was killed.

※レース終了後の晩、タムラ・アベンジは謎の騎航を行い、クラッシュ。全壊した。　騎手は皇路操であったと思われるが、この日以降、彼女の消息は不明。
On the night after the race, the Tamura Avenger made a mysterious crafting maneuver and crashed. She was completely destroyed.　 It is believed that Ouji Misao was the crafter, but her whereabouts have been unknown since that day.

またほぼ同時刻、タムラのガレージでメカニックの一人が死亡している。　しかしこれについて警察からもタムラからも公的な発表はなく、彼の氏名ほかの素性は明らかでない。
At about the same time, one of the mechanics was killed in Tamura's garage.　However, neither the police nor Tamura made any public announcement about this, and his name and other details are not known.

※上記の事件については様々な憶測が飛び交い、一々記す事もできない。また大半は荒唐無稽なものである。　だが、大和ＧＰの背後に装甲競技賭博化を巡る抗争があったことはほぼ事実とみられ、
There is so much speculation about the above incidents that it is impossible to write about them all. Most of them are ridiculous.　However, it seems to be almost a fact that there was a war over the gambling of armored competition behind the Yamato GP.

翔京がこれを進め、タムラがこれに反対していた事も、複数の関係者が私的な発言で明らかにしている。
Several sources have revealed in private statements that Shokyo was pushing for this and Tamura was opposed to it.

賭博化について愛好者の間では賛否両論だが、大和ＧＰにおける皇路操とアベンジの騎航は既に半ば伝説的であり、あの騎影に想いを寄せ再来を願う風潮は党派の枠を超えて強く――
While there's a lot of controversy among enthusiasts about the idea of gambling, the crafting of Ouji Misao and Avenge in the Yamato GP is already half-legendary, and there's a strong tendency across party lines to think about the shadow of that craft and hope for its return.

彼らはタムラの姿勢に協調、結集して賭博化反対の宣言を行い、徹底抗戦の構えを見せている。　大和ＧＰで敗れた翔京が賭博化をいまだ断念していないとしても、実現は困難を極めるであろう…………
They are cooperating with Tamura's stance, rallying together to declare their opposition to gambling, and are prepared to fight tooth and nail.　Even if Shogyo, who lost the Yamato GP, has not yet given up on the idea of gambling, it will be extremely difficult to realize. ............

愛するセシリーへ
To my dear Cecily.

あるいは体は健康でも、何か他の心配事があったりはしないだろうか。そのような時にはフロリダの母を頼って欲しい。
Or maybe you are in good health, but have something else to worry about. In such cases, I hope you will turn to my mother in Florida.

ああ、だが僕は何を言っているのだろう。これほど君の身を案じているのだから、今すぐに忌々しい海を越えて帰り、この両腕で君を抱きかかえて、あらゆる害悪から守るべきであるのに。君は僕がそうしない事について、大いなる失望を禁じ得ないのではないか？僕の愛情の不足に確信を持ってしまうのではないか？
Oh, but what am I saying? Since I care for you so much, I should go back home across the dreadful sea right now and hold you in my arms and protect you from all harm. You can't help but be very disappointed that I don't do that, can you? Wouldn't you be convinced of my lack of love?

だから僕は君との一時的な別離を受け入れ、異教の劣等人種を相手とする任務に従事している。何と気の滅入る日々であることか。
So I have accepted my temporary separation from you and am on a mission against a pagan inferior race. What depressing days these are.

小さなダニーにもどうか教えておいて欲しい。

It is said that the game between musha and musha is determined mainly by the following four factors.　The four main factors are ascent performance, maximum speed, acceleration performance, and turning performance.

上昇性能の重大さは論を俟つまい。　戦闘開始時における高度優勢の確保はこの能力如何だ。
The importance of climb performance cannot be overstated.　Securing altitude superiority at the start of a battle depends on this capability.

After the initial collision, it depends on your turning performance.　The quicker you can turn, the easier it is to gain altitude advantage.

Maximum speed is the most important factor in determining the power of the first attack in a match.　A superior speed means that you can strike a more powerful blow before the enemy.

そして加速性能は、二合目以降の速力を左右する。　激突で減殺された速力の回復は、この性能に懸かる。

There is no such thing as a craft that has all four of these abilities perfectly.　This is because the pursuit of one kind of ability is often inseparable from the reduction of another kind of ability.

翼甲を拡大すれば旋回性が増し加速性が失われる。　翼甲を分厚く強固にすれば最大速力は高まるが上昇性能は犠牲になる。
Enlarging the wing armor will increase turning performance and reduce acceleration.　If the wing armor is thicker and stronger, the maximum speed will be increased, but the climbing performance will be sacrificed.

Vertical inversion.　This is a feat that can only be accomplished by grasping and utilizing the occurrence of falling gravity at the moment when the ascent speed is reduced to nothing.

〝金翅鳥王剣〟
"Golden-winged Bird King Ken

マックス・インメルマン中尉。　外暦一九一四年から一九一八年にわたって戦われた欧州戦争において、比類なき勇名を鳴り響かせた独逸の誇る撃墜王の一人である。
Lieutenant Max Immelmann.　He was one of Germany's proudest shot-down kings who made a name for himself with his unparalleled bravery during the European War fought from 1914 to 1918.

その名に〝侯〟の一語が無い事からも明らかな通り、彼は竜騎兵団に属してはいたものの、騎士階級の出身ではなかった。　真打劔冑の継承者ではなかったのである。
Although he was a member of the Dragon Craft Corps, he was not from the crafting class, as evidenced by the absence of the word "lord" in his name.　He was not the heir to the "Shin-uchi tsurugi*".

この時代の撃墜王としては異例と云わねばならない。　外暦一九〇〇年代初頭（国紀二五〇〇年代中盤）はまだ数打劔冑が開発されて間もない頃であり、現在に比べれば性能は著しく低いレベルに留まっていた。
I must say that this is unusual for a downed king of this era.　In the early 1900's (mid 1950's), the tsurugi* had just been developed, and its performance was still remarkably low compared to today.

彼が愛騎としたフォッカーＥ３とてもそうだ。　張線支持を採用した単翼騎――当時代の技術の粋が凝らされた騎体ではあったが、真打劔冑との性能差を埋めるものでは到底ない。
The Fokker E3, which he considered his favorite craft, is no different.　It was a single-wing craft with taut-wire support - a craft body that incorporated the best of the technology of the time, but it was far from enough to make up for the difference in performance of the Tsurugi*-tono.

その頃、戦場に華を添えた各国の撃墜王――由緒正しい名門の騎士であり最高の劔冑を継承していた人々――と、一介の騎兵将校インメルマンとの間に、騎体性能の点で巨大な隔絶があったことは確実である。
It is certain that there was a huge gap in terms of craft performance between the shoot-down kings of various countries who added their splendor to the battlefield at that time - the venerable and prestigious craftmen who had inherited the highest tsurugi* - and Immelmann, a simple craft officer.

しかも、彼の配属された北フランス戦線は敵に正規の騎士が多く、対して味方の騎士は大半が対露戦線に派遣されていたためほとんど皆無という、実に苛酷を極める状況下にあった。

味方は彼を含めて新弱の竜騎兵ばかり。　敵方は古強の騎士が居並ぶ。　……武功を掲げるどころか、生き残るだけでも至難であったに違いない。
He and his teammates are all new and weak dragon crafters.　I'm not sure what to make of it.　In the event that you've got a lot of time and energy, you'll be able to take advantage of it.

その死線にあってインメルマンを撃墜王たらしめたのは、少年期に出会った異国人との体験だった。
What made Immelmann the king of shooting down the enemy was an experience he had with a foreigner when he was a boy.

徳川時代の幕引き後、大和はやや閉鎖的であった前時代の反動のように西洋文化を多く取り入れ、何それとなく学んだが、軍事編制においてはプロイセン――ドイツに倣う所が非常に多かった。
After the end of the Tokugawa era, Yamato adopted a lot of Western culture as a reaction to the previous era, which had been somewhat closed off, and learned more than a few things.

プロイセン軍こそ欧州最精強と見る向きが強かったためである。　幾度となく軍事交流団が派遣され、貪欲に技術知識を求めた。
This was because the Prussian army was considered by many to be the strongest in Europe.　The Prussian army was seen by many as the most powerful in Europe, and military exchange delegations were dispatched many times, greedily seeking technical knowledge.

日向守異聞　　　　　　　　第四七回　信貴山落城
Hyuga Mamoru Anecdotes 47th Nobukeyama Castle

〝――ついに織田が手勢は大手門を打ち破り、怒涛となつて城内へ雪崩れ込む。　一気呵成と押し寄せる人馬に右衛門佐少しも怯まず立ちはだかるも、多勢に無勢、ここに窮まり〟
"At last, Oda's forces broke through the main gate and avalanched into the castle in a rage.　They were outnumbered and outgunned.

〝三人四人と突き伏せて、なお次なる敵を求めて頭を巡らす右衛門佐、恐れたじろぐ織田の兵陣からひとり駆け出でた惟任日向が家来佐々木某に槍を打ち折られ〟
"Uemonsa, who had pushed three or four men to the ground and was still searching for the next enemy, rushed out alone from the fearful ranks of the Oda soldiers, but his spear was broken by a certain Sasaki, his retainer.

〝太刀抜く間もあればこそ、今なりと次々槍さす雑兵輩、腹に肩にと矛先を受け、松永が嫡子の命運尽くる。　佐々木某その首落とし、右衛門佐久通かくして果てたり。享年三五、辞世は無しと伝えらる〟
"It is only now, when I have time to draw my sword, that I am speared, one after another, in the belly and shoulder, and the fate of Matsunaga's legitimate son is ended.　A certain Sasaki lost his head, and Hisamichi Uemonsa died in this way. It is said that he died at the age of 35 without dying.

〝右衛門佐斃ると知るや、篭城方は足並み乱れ、旗幟を変えて槍先転ずる者、鎧兜を脱ぎ捨てて遁走する者後を絶たず、攻城方が二の丸三の丸に火を放てば意気地ある者も観念し、自ら害してせめて骸を敵に渡さず〟
"As soon as they learned that Uemonsa was dying, the siege forces fell into disarray, and there was no end to the number of those who changed their banners and turned their spears, or took off their armor and fled.

〝やんぬるかな松永弾正忠、この始末を本丸上頂より見下ろして、最期の時来るを悟りけり。　雲霞の如き眼下の軍勢、総大将は憎みても憎き信長が嫡男秋田城介、その馬印を見取つて歯を打ち鳴らし〟
"As he looked down from the top of the Honmaru, he realized that the time of his death had come.　The army below was like a haze of clouds, and the commander-in-chief was Nobunaga's legitimate son, Akita Jousuke, whom he hated even more than he hated him, looking at his horse's mark and clicking his teeth.

〝敗亡はよし、死すもよし、なれど一矢も報いずには済ませまいと、弾正茶釜を抱え上げ、織田の者どもの目にさらす。　秋田城介思わず立ち、傍らの羽柴筑前も泡を食う〟
"It's all right to lose, it's all right to die, but I'm not going to let it go unpunished," he said, holding up the Danjo tea kettle and exposing it to the eyes of the Oda men.　It's a good thing I'm dead, but I'm not going to let this go unanswered.

〝這いつくばりたる蜘蛛にも似たその異形の茶釜こそ、織田内府かねて所望の大名物。　謀叛二度に渡る松永を、これと引き換えに赦免すとまで内府をして言わしめたる〟
"This oddly shaped tea kettle, resembling a spider crawling on its back, is the great treasure that the Oda household has long desired.　It has even been used to pardon Matsunaga, who rebelled twice, in exchange for it.

〝慌てふためき制止の声を張り上げる秋田城介、弾正応じず高らかに嘲り笑うと、末期の一句を詠じたり〟　〝――だるぶし、あどぅら、うる、ばあくる――〟

〝その一句が付け火となりしか。　途方もなき爆発が城郭を揺るがし、辺りを噴煙の下に埋め尽くす〟

"A cloud of smoke is gradually clearing, and in its place appears a huge shape.　Its appearance resembles that of a crawling spider, and it is no less than a tea kettle.

〝しかし身の丈は山の如く膨れ上がり、まさしく天を突かんばかり。　茶釜の上に仁王立つは言わずと知れた松永弾正忠、諸手を上げて息を吸うなり、大音声にて宣告す〟

Since that rainy day.

But then again, there are other ways to spend your time.　He didn't have to spend day after day throwing unwarranted accusations at the garden plants.

ほとんど役には立たぬにしても、村正の探索行動を手伝うとか。　銀星号との対決に備え、日課の鍛錬の量を増やしてみるとか。
